Even though a long time has passed since our romantic relationship ended, it's curious that they continues to give me lessons that encourage me to grow. Although, it was also terribly painful to notice that we don't even function as friends, we are not made to have contact because we are both in very different moments of our lives, in fact we are in different books. I just want to remember it for what it was, a normal relationship with the good, the bad and the ugly, and filled with many teachings, with a lot of emotional growth. This song came out right when I needed it to. My ex and I have been in a very rough relationship. We dated for two years, and he cheated on me two times. I never forgave him but I still let him stay with me because I hoped he would change. Other than the cheating, he was really abusive & we turned into a long distance relationship after I moved back home. He's currently abroad working & we talk daily. He's super apologetic about the way he cheated on me but the cycle of abuse he constantly puts me in is him getting angry at me for the little things, hanging up on me or telling me to fuck off, and then him calling back or texting me saying that he's sorry. I used to resent him so much for every time he hurt me that I would think to myself that if I wasn't happy then he didn't deserve to be either. I don't know why I was so madly in love with him because maybe it was just me telling myself that I was in love with who he used to be. After a huge argument between me and him, I just stopped loving him all together. I was too attached to break it off officially, but it took so much out of me to do it. I resented him so much because he told me that I treated him like shit and that everything was my fault for him "hurting" (his friends cut him off because of how shitty he was to me). He would suicide bait me, telling me that he hated himself and he self-harmed because he hated how he "treated" me. I hated him but I was scared of him hurting himself. After I broke up with him, I had to cut him off and let go. I was still so attached, but I learned to stop myself from reaching out to him ever again. This song spoke to me in a spiritual level and kinda told me the message that I need peace. I wish him well, because that's just how I am. I hope me and him never cross paths again, but I hope he lives life like how I will live mine.

No fights, no toxicity, no hard feelings... we just grew apart. I wish you roses
At this rate, I am just going to buy/listen to her music while trying hard not to look at any of her covers or music videos. Kali is an immensely talented R&B and pop songwriter/singer, and her past two albums are a testament to that claim, but all the in-your-face-full-frontal-nudity is just distracting and something I have come to expect from her since Telepatia. Regardless of gender, this level of "body art" is just too much and unnecessary. Sensuality and sex appeal does not always have to come in the form of risque nudity - just look at Sade! The makeup is gorgeous here, the melody is languorous yet sensual, the lyrics are heart-wrenching and the avant-garde rose costume with the petal headdress is inventive - I wish she had kept things at that. But if this is the kind of attention she enjoys, then to each his/her own.
